All UTF-8 characters
Every 20 characters, an index is printed so you can figure the correct entity code. Just count backwards from the ( index ) number on same row as your character, and subtract that from the index number to get the correct &#1234; code. If you see question marks it's because the Microsoft-supplied unicode font set does not know how to render every UTF-8 character in existence.
